Sub: Submission of the 39th Annual Report for the year 2024-25 
 
Dear Sir / Madam, 
 
 
Pursuant to Regulation 34(1) of SEBI (Listing Obligations and Disclosure Requirements) Regulations, 
2015, please find attached the 39th Annual Report of the Company for the financial year 2024-25 
containing therein the Notice of the Annual General Meeting to be held on Thursday, 6th November, 
2025 at 10.30 a.m. through video conferencing mode. 
 
Today, the Company, through the electronic mode has initiated the process to send the Annual Report 
along with the Notice of the 39th Annual General Meeting to those Members whose name was 
recorded in the Register of Members or in the Register of Beneficial Owners maintained by the 
Depositories as of Friday, 3rd October 2025. 
 
The Annual Report is in the process of uploading on the website of the Company - 
(https://w3.accelya.com/investors). 
 
We request you to take the same on your records. 
 
 
Thanking you,  
 For Accelya Solutions India Limited  
 
 
Ninad Umranikar  
Company Secretary

are adhered to across all vendors and suppliers engaged in various locations. The Company ensured that all office 
stationery materials were sourced from authorized suppliers, ensuring compliance with regulatory guidelines.
